DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  # Set environment variables for non-interactive installs and UTF-8
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # (Optional) Create a non-root user 'cc' and adjust permissions (commented out; enable if needed)
  # RUN useradd -ms /bin/bash cc
  # USER cc
  # Copy project files (assumes files are in build context)
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then chmod +x install.sh; fi
  # Install Python dependencies via requirements.txt if present, else via install.sh or pip
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install -r requirements.txt ; \
      elif [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          ./install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  # Install Jupyter Notebook (optional, for interactive use)
  RUN pip install notebook
  # Install CmdStan (latest stable) into /opt/cmdstan; add to PATH
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  # Set permissions for the cc user (optional, if using USER cc)
  # RUN chown -R cc:cc /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Set default entrypoint to bash for development, or override in docker-compose or command line
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Set environment variables for non-interactive installs and UTF-8
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # (Optional) Create a non-root user 'cc' and adjust permissions (commented out; enable if needed)
  # RUN useradd -ms /bin/bash cc
  # USER cc
  # Copy project files (assumes files are in build context)
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then chmod +x install.sh; fi
  # Verify presence and permissions of requirements.txt and install.sh
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Install Python dependencies via install.sh if present, else via pip
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          ./install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  # Install Jupyter Notebook (optional, for interactive use)
  RUN pip install notebook
  # Install CmdStan (latest stable) into /opt/cmdstan; add to PATH
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  # Set permissions for the cc user (optional, if using USER cc)
  # RUN chown -R cc:cc /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Set default entrypoint to bash for development, or override in docker-compose or command line
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Set environment variables for non-interactive installs and UTF-8
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # (Optional) Create a non-root user 'cc' and adjust permissions (commented out; enable if needed)
  # RUN useradd -ms /bin/bash cc
  # USER cc
  # Copy project files (assumes files are in build context)
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then chmod +x install.sh; fi
  # Verify presence and permissions of requirements.txt and install.sh
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Install Python dependencies via install.sh if present, else via pip
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          bash install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  # Install Jupyter Notebook (optional, for interactive use)
  RUN pip install notebook
  # Install CmdStan (latest stable) into /opt/cmdstan; add to PATH
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  # Set permissions for the cc user (optional, if using USER cc)
  # RUN chown -R cc:cc /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Set default entrypoint to bash for development, or override in docker-compose or command line
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 4 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh uses Unix line endings, has a valid shebang, and is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          dos2unix install.sh && \
          grep -q '^#!' install.sh || (sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh); \
          chmod +x install.sh; \
      fi
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Run install.sh if present, fallback to pip if not
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          bash install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh uses Unix line endings, has a valid shebang, and is executable if present
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          dos2unix install.sh && \
          grep -q '^#!' install.sh || (sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh); \
          chmod +x install.sh; \
      fi
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz && \
      if [ -f install.sh ]; then cat install.sh; fi
  # Run install.sh if present, fallback to pip if not
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          ./install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Run install.sh atomically if present, fallback to pip if not
  RUN if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          dos2unix install.sh && \
          grep -q '^#!' install.sh || (sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh); \
          chmod +x install.sh && \
          ./install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Run install.sh atomically if present, fallback to pip if not, with debug output and explicit interpreter
  RUN set -x && \
      if [ -f install.sh ]; then \
          dos2unix install.sh && \
          grep -q '^#!' install.sh || (sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh); \
          chmod +x install.sh && \
          /bin/bash install.sh ; \
      else \
          pip install --upgrade pip && \
          pip install numpy scipy pandas tqdm pystan pyro-ppl edward tensorflow==1.15 ; \
      fi
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh has correct line endings and shebang, then run it
  RUN dos2unix install.sh && \
      (head -n 1 install.sh | grep -q '^#!' || sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh) && \
      chmod +x install.sh && \
      /bin/bash install.sh
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN ls -l /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Debug: Show contents of install.sh before running
  RUN dos2unix install.sh && \
      (head -n 1 install.sh | grep -q '^#!' || sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh) && \
      chmod +x install.sh && \
      cat install.sh
  # Run install.sh with bash -x for detailed debug output
  RUN /bin/bash -x install.sh
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz

      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          python3-pip \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

      ln -sf /usr/local/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip

  RUN dos2unix install.sh && \
      (head -n 1 install.sh | grep -q '^#!' || sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh) && \
      chmod +x install.sh && \
      cat install.sh
  # Debug: Ensure pip is available before running install.sh
  RUN which pip && pip --version
  # Run install.sh with bash -x for detailed debug output
  RUN /bin/bash -x install.sh
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 11 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          python3-pip \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN ln -sf /usr/local/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Ensure install.sh has Unix line endings and a valid shebang
  RUN if [ ! -f install.sh ]; then echo "install.sh missing!"; exit 1; fi && \
      dos2unix install.sh && \
      (head -n 1 install.sh | grep -q '^#!' || sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh) && \
      chmod +x install.sh
  RUN which pip && pip --version
  RUN bash ./install.sh
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          python3-pip \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN ln -sf /usr/local/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Fix install.sh: Unix line endings, valid shebang, executable; print content for debug
  RUN if [ ! -f install.sh ]; then echo "install.sh missing!"; exit 1; fi && \
      dos2unix install.sh && \
      (head -n 1 install.sh | grep -q '^#!' || sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh) && \
      chmod +x install.sh && \
      echo "===== install.sh content below =====" && head -n 20 install.sh
  RUN which pip && pip --version
  # Run with explicit bash path and print debug output if fails
  RUN /bin/bash -x ./install.sh || (echo "install.sh failed, printing its content:" && cat ./install.sh && exit 1)
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM python:3.8-slim
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          ca-certificates \
          bash \
          make \
          g++ \
          jq \
          python3-venv \
          dos2unix \
          python3-pip \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN ln -sf /usr/local/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/python && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/bin/pip3 /usr/local/bin/pip
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/probfuzz
  # Fix install.sh: Unix line endings, valid shebang, executable; print content for debug
  RUN if [ ! -f install.sh ]; then echo "install.sh missing!"; exit 1; fi && \
      dos2unix install.sh && \
      (head -n 1 install.sh | grep -q '^#!' || sed -i '1i #!/bin/bash' install.sh) && \
      chmod +x install.sh && \
      echo "===== install.sh content below =====" && cat install.sh
  RUN which pip && pip --version
  # Enhanced debug: capture install.sh output and always print on failure
  RUN set -e; \
      { /bin/bash -x ./install.sh 2>&1 | tee install.log; } || { \
        echo "===== install.sh failed, printing its content ====="; \
        cat ./install.sh; \
        echo "===== install.log output below ====="; \
        cat install.log; \
        exit 1; \
      }
  RUN pip install notebook
  ENV CMDSTAN_VERSION=2.33.1
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      cd /opt && \
      wget https://github.com/stan-dev/cmdstan/releases/download/v${CMDSTAN_VERSION}/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      rm cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}.tar.gz && \
      cd cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION} && \
      make build -j"$(nproc)"
  ENV PATH="/opt/cmdstan-${CMDSTAN_VERSION}:${PATH}"
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
